## Analysis

The Ground Truth (GT) expression is:
$$f(t, A) = -0.15728 \cdot A + 0.49114 \cdot \sin(\log(A + 1))$$

Note that the GT has no dependence on `t` (since `c1 * _t` = 0.15728 * 3.12275 ≈ 0.49114, and `_t` is a fixed constant absorbed into the coefficient). So the GT is effectively:

$$f(A) = c_a \cdot A + c_b \cdot \sin(\log(A + 1))$$

where $c_a = -0.15728$ and $c_b = 0.49114$.

Now I need to find candidates that can express this form: a linear term in A plus a sin(log(A+1)) term, with all other terms vanishing.

**Candidate 6**: `A*c0 + c1*exp(c2/(c3 + t)) + c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7)`

Setting:
- c0 = -0.15728 (linear A term)
- c1 = 0 (kills the exp term, removing t-dependence)
- c4 = 0.49114
- c5 = 1 (so we get log(A*c6 + 1))
- c6 = 1 (so we get log(A + 1))
- c7 = 0 (no phase shift)

This gives: $-0.15728 \cdot A + 0.49114 \cdot \sin(\log(A + 1))$ ✓

**Candidate 33**: `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2*exp(c3/(c4 + t)) + c5 + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)`

Setting c0 = 0, c1 = -0.15728, c2 = 0, c5 = 0, c6 = 0.49114, c7 = 1, c8 = 1, c9 = 0. This also works. ✓

**Candidate 10**: `A**2*c0 + A**c1*c2 + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)`

Setting c0 = 0, c1 = 1 (so A**c1 = A), c2 = -0.15728, c3 = 0, c4 = 0, c6 = 0.49114, c7 = 1, c8 = 1, c9 = 0. This works. ✓

**Candidate 47**: `A**2*c0 + A**2*c1/(A + c2)**2 + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)`

Setting c0 = 0, c1 = 0 (or arranging the rational term to give a linear A term is complex), c4 = 0, c3 = 0... Actually, we can set c1 = 0 to kill the rational term, but then we lose the linear A term. We need `A**2*c0 + A**2*c1/(A+c2)**2` to produce a linear term in A. This is more complex but possible with specific parameter choices (though tricky). Let me note this is less clean.

**Candidate 35**: `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*exp(A**c3*c4) + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8)`

Setting c1 = 0 (so exp(0) = 1, giving c0*A), c0 = -0.15728, c2 = 0 (kills exp term), c5 = 0.49114, c6 = 1, c7 = 1, c8 = 0. This works. ✓

Multiple candidates match. The clearest match is **Candidate 6**.
